      "type": "User",
      "site_admin": false
    },
    "body": "Since 1.20.30, it is possible to send clients a link to download a resource pack from - instead of having to add the pack to Geyser's pack folder. This should help with proxy networks & overall traffic usage, as now resource intensive pack sending can be offloaded to a designated location. However, unlike on Java, it is possible to send multiple entries for the client to load packs from!\r\n\r\nNotes:\r\n- This will only work on 1.20.30 and up. A workaround can be to block all versions below using the [BlockVersion](https://github.com/onebeastchris/BlockVersion) extension. ~~Or, an extension/a plugin could manually query the Bedrock client version and add either a link, or a pack (depending on version).~~ Update: If the client fails at getting the packs from the url, or does not support the entries, it will request the packs the old way.\r\n\r\nChanges:\r\n- add new `GeyserUrlPackCodec` (and `UrlPackCodec` for api) that can create a pack based on url + content key\r\n- add a `resource-pack-urls` entry in the config for remote packs\r\n- try and use more fastutil for resource packs\r\n\r\nRFC:\r\n- ~~Should users be able to set pack encryption keys for the url's in the config?~~ No, users should use api instead for that.\r\n- ~~What should be done if the link stops working (e.g. because packs do not actually provide the correct pack anymore? Should Geyser then attempt to reload all packs (or just the remote packs)?~~ Geyser will then serve the cached pack, and re-run a check of the url once - and warn about it.\n\r\nWe can detect it if the client sends a `ResourcePackChunkRequestPacket` - if the pack requested there is one with the UrlPackCodec, we can assume that either ~~1. the client does not support remote pack~~ to my knowledge , all platforms now do, or that 2. the remote pack changed/an error occurred/etc and that Geyser might want to re-check it.\r\nHowever, it is not currently possible to modify registry contents, which makes that a bit more challenging. \r\n-  ~~Should Geyser download the remote packs once and provide that, or should Geyser rather try and get it directly from the url?~~ We'll be downloading the pack once, and cache it to avoid unnecessary re-downloads\r\n\r\nTODO:\r\n- [x] Testing; more of it\r\n- [x] javadocs spellchecks\r\n- [x] Proper error handling: URL invalid/offline, corrupt pack, manifest not where it's supposed to be, etc. \r\n- [x] documentation on wiki\r\n- [x] remove debug\r\n- [x] dont let resource pack downloading block main thread - this is actually wanted; since Geyser should not start before we know all the resource packs\r\n- [x] Don't re-download the pack if there's no need to (hash from url + size)\r\n\r\nWould close https://github.com/GeyserMC/Geyser/issues/4060 - atleast the resource pack part.                                         ",

    "body": "## todo:\r\n- [x] the lack of permissions on standalone. what this causes needs to be cleaned up, at least in extension commands.\r\n- [x] create `permissions.yml` file for standalone\r\n- [x] remove standalone permission hacks from builtin cmmands\r\n- [x] `isSuggestedOpOnly` is kind of problematic imo, in regards to its wording and the way it is used. it can probably just be deprecated in favour of optional permission registration\r\n\r\n - [x] properly handle stopping execution due to `isExecutableOnConsole` or `isBedrockOnly` with descriptive messages\r\n - [x] exceptions are completely unhandled on Geyser-Standalone right now\r\n - [x] convert builtin commands to fully utilize cloud features\r\n - [x] fix senderType\r\n - [x] pretty sure just `/geyser` is suppose to send help?\r\n - [x] exception handlers needs to be overriden on every platform (except standalone i guess) so that messages can be properly localized\r\n - [x] localize all messages\r\n - [x] deal with possible trailing whitespace on geyser standalone gui \r\n - [x] java players get suggested bedrock only commands -> additionally add platform check as a permission predicate\r\n - [x] restore Spigot COMMAND_MAP lookup for descriptions\r\n - [x] search CommandRegistry for our own description(s)\r\n - [x] javadocs\r\n - [x] check if we need to strip trailing whitespace before dispatching to cloud from BedrockCommandRequestTranslator (when Geyser Standalone is in use)\r\n - [x] fix certain commands not working properly with `handleNoPermission`\r\n - [ ] i think `command.failed` lang might be broken\r\n\r\n## future and separate PRs\r\n- implementations of CommandSource#sendMessage are wildly different in terms of what kind of text format is passed to it. maybe an earlier PR.\r\n- use cloud's brigadier mappings to get suggestions on geyser standalone\r\n- add tab completion to geyser standalone JLine\r\n\r\n## changes\r\n\r\n- `GeyserCommandManager` has been renamed to `CommandRegistry`\r\n- `GeyserCommandExecutor` and all subclasses have been removed in favour of Cloud.\r\n- `WorldManager#hasPermission` has been removed in favour of Cloud.\r\n\r\n- Spigot\r\n  - no longer depends on paper mojang api.\r\n  - `GeyserBrigadierSupport` has been removed in favour of Cloud.\r\n  - [GeyserPaperCommandListener](https://github.com/GeyserMC/Geyser/pull/3808/files#diff-0dea5ed4c55d5c72d8261cf376f20157eaf6e56b10e32df1b84ecdcb3a58887e) has been removed - cloud (and the way i designed permission checks) handles what it did.\r\n\r\n- Standalone:\r\n  - `permissions.yml` has been added, a list of default permissions available to all players.\r\n\r\n- Velocity/BungeeCord/Fabric/Standalone: commands are now registered before `GeyserPostInitializeEvent`, for consistency with Spigot, and to allow valid registration on Fabric.\r\n  - There is still inconsistency between bootstraps on whether or not commands are re-registered whenever a reload occurs.\r\n\r\n## api changes:\r\n\r\n### deprecations\r\n- `Command#isSuggestedOpOnly` and the relevant builder method have been deprecated for removal\r\n- `Command#subCommands` has been deprecated for removal and will always return `Collections.emptyList()`\r\n- `Command#isExecutableOnConsole()` has been deprecated & replaced with `#isPlayerOnly()`\r\n### changes\r\n- `Command#aliases()` now always returns an immutable list\r\n\r\n### additions\r\n- `Command.Builder#permission(String, Tristate)` - register the permission and its default value to the server implementation if possible.\r\n- `CommandSource#playerUuid` - return a uuid if the source represents a player.\r\n- `CommandSource#connection` - return a Connection if the source represents a bedrock player managed by the current Geyser instance.\r\n---\r\n- `GeyserRegisterPermissionCheckersEvent` - only used by Geyser-Standalone. Fired when the command manager is created. Allows registering `PermissionChecker`s to the manager. Event listeners with a higher listener priority will register PermissionCheckers as having a higher priority.\r\n- `PermissionChecker` - api interface that is responsible for resolving a CommandSource and a permission node to a Tristate.\r\n---\r\n- `GeyserRegisterPermissionsEvent` - fired by a server platform, or extension, or anything, when it is the proper time for permissions to be registered to the event caller. This event will be called by Geyser-Spigot/Standalone/Forge. An extension may also fire the event in order to register permissions to LuckPerms for Geyser-Velocity/BungeeCord/Fabric. Geyser's CommandRegistry will listen for this event, but api users may as well.",

    "body": "The server only started sending its render distance during 1.14. ViaVersion compensates by sending 64 as the render distance, always - but this can choke up Bedrock in various ways. This PR fixes two separate issues related:\r\n\r\n- In some instances, the client would be stuck on Building Terrain during server switch. This is solved by fake-decreasing the render distance during server transfer. Zero issues have been found thus far.\r\n- When switching servers, chunks could be dropped. While not pretty, if the client is not spawned, they are teleported to near the chunks so they cannot be unloaded.",

I'm no expert in collisions, however; I have to thank `pokechu22` for giving me some excellent reference code to work with.\r\n\r\nUnlike fishing rod pulling behavior that is calculated serverside on Bedrock and clientside on Java, Bedrock player \"pushing\" is nonexistent on Bedrock. This code checks to see if a Geyser player should be moved, and if so applies motion to the player which sends movement packets back.\r\n\r\nThis commit also cleans up the move relative code of villagers so they aren't always checking the chunk cache.",
